    <equation xml:id="S0.Ex7">
      <Math mode="display" tex="\begin{array}[]{rcl}\delta(b_{i}b_{j})&amp;=&amp;s_{0i}s_{0j}\sum\limits_{k}N_{ijk}%&#10;\delta(\tilde{b_{k}})\\&#10;&amp;=&amp;s_{0i}s_{0j}[\dfrac{s_{0i}s_{0j}}{d_{0}}\sum\limits^{r-1}_{k=0}\bar{s}_{0k}%&#10;s_{0k}]+s_{0i}s_{0j}[\sum\limits^{r-1}_{l=1}\dfrac{s_{li}s_{lj}}{d_{l}}\sum%&#10;\limits^{r-1}_{k=0}\bar{s}_{lk}s_{0k}]\\&#10;&amp;=&amp;s_{0i}s_{0j}[\dfrac{s_{0i}s_{0j}}{d_{0}}d_{0}]+s_{0i}s_{0j}[0]\\&#10;&amp;=&amp;s^{2}_{0i}s^{2}_{0j}=\delta(b_{i})\delta(b_{j})\end{array}" text="Array[[delta * b _ i * b _ j, =, s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j) * (sum _ k)@(N _ (i * j * k) * delta * tilde@(b _ k))], [, =, s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j) * delimited-[]@(((s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j)) / d _ 0) * ((sum ^ (r - 1)) _ (k = 0))@((bar@(s)) _ (0 * k) * s _ (0 * k))) + s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j) * delimited-[]@(((sum ^ (r - 1)) _ (l = 1))@(((s _ (l * i) * s _ (l * j)) / d _ l) * ((sum ^ (r - 1)) _ (k = 0))@((bar@(s)) _ (l * k) * s _ (0 * k))))], [, =, s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j) * delimited-[]@(((s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j)) / d _ 0) * d _ 0) + s _ (0 * i) * s _ (0 * j) * delimited-[]@(0)], [, =, (s ^ 2) _ (0 * i) * (s ^ 2) _ (0 * j) = delta * b _ i * delta * b _ j]]" xml:id="S0.Ex7.m1">
